[Thought: true]I have found the absolute root cause. 

The `AuthProvider` component, which was added in the broken commit `75ad9c22`, is the culprit. In the stable version (`ff864710`), there was **no AuthProvider**. Instead, every page was "self-sufficient"—it managed its own `session` state and checked Supabase directly. 

When we centralized Auth into a single Provider, we created a single point of failure that the mobile WebView (which freezes JavaScript) couldn't handle correctly on resume.

### The "Back to Basics" Stability Plan (v1.18.10)
I am going to perform a true surgical restoration of the 1.18.1 architecture:

1.  **Delete `AuthProvider.tsx`:** We are removing the component that introduced the instability.
2.  **Restore `Layout.tsx`:** Remove the `<AuthProvider>` wrapper so pages are independent again.
3.  **Self-Sufficient Pages:** Update Home, Predict, Leaderboard, and Leagues to manage their own `session` state using `supabase.auth.getSession()` inside their `init()` functions (exactly like the stable 1.18.1 version).
4.  **Keep the Best Fixes:** I will still use the standard `@supabase/supabase-js` client (more reliable than SSR) and keep the `withTimeout` / `mountedRef` safety checks.

**This is the most aggressive and definitive way to restore the "webpage" and "mobile" stability you had in 1.18.1.**

Shall I proceed with removing the AuthProvider and restoring page independence? (v1.18.10)

Load from cache first\n    const cachedRace = localStorage.getItem('p10_cache_next_race');\n    const cachedDrivers = localStorage.getItem('p10_cache_drivers');\n    \n    if (cachedRace && mountedRef.current) {\n      try {\n        const raceData = JSON.parse(cachedRace);\n        setNextRace(raceData);\n        \n        const now = new Date().getTime();\n        const targetStr = `${raceData.date}T${raceData.time}`;\n        const target = new Date(targetStr).getTime();\n        const distance = target - now;\n        const fourHoursLater = target + 4 * 60 * 60 * 1000;\n\n        if (distance < 0 && mountedRef.current) {\n          setShowCountdown(false);\n          setIsRaceInProgress(now < fourHoursLater);\n        } else if (mountedRef.current) {\n          setShowCountdown(true);\n          setIsRaceInProgress(false);\n          setCountdown({\n            d: Math.floor(distance / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)),\n            h: Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) / (1000 * 60 * 60)),\n            m: Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60)) / (1000 * 60)),\n            s: Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60)) / 1000)\n          });\n        }\n      } catch (e) { console.error('Cache parse error', e); }\n    }\n    \n    if (cachedDrivers && mountedRef.current) setAllDrivers(JSON.parse(cachedDrivers));\n\n    if (!cachedRace && mountedRef.current) {\n      setLoading(true);\n    }\n\n    try {\n      // 2. finalized = localStorage.getItem(`final_pred_${CURRENT_SEASON}_${name}_${nextRace.id}`);\n    if (finalized) {\n      const parsed = JSON.parse(finalized);\n      setP10Driver(parsed.p10);\n      setDnfDriver(parsed.dnf);\n    } else {\n      setP10Driver('');\n      setDnfDriver('');\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleGuestLogin = (e: React.FormEvent) => {\n    e.preventDefault();\n    Haptics.impact({ style: ImpactStyle.Medium });\n    const cleanName = tempUsername.trim();\n    if (cleanName.length >= 3) {\n      selectUser(cleanName);\n    } else {\n      showNotification('Name setUsername('');\n    setTempUsername('');\n  };\n\n  const handleShare = async () => {\n    if (!nextRace) return;\n    const p10Name = getDriverDisplayName(p10Driver, drivers as Driver[]);\n    const dnfName = getDriverDisplayName(dnfDriver, drivers as Driver[]);\n    const text = `🏎️ My P10 Racing Picks for the ${nextRace.name}!\\n\\n🎯 P10 Finisher: ${p10Name}\\n🔥 First DNF: ${dnfName}\\n\\nCan you master the midfield? #P10Racing #F1`;\n    \n    try {\n      await Share.share({\n        title: 'P10 Racing Predictions',\n        text: text,\n        url: 'https://p10racing.app/predict',\n        dialogTitle: 'Share your Picks',\n      });\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.log('Share dismissed or failed:', error);\n      if (!navigator.share && navigator.clipboard) {\n        navigator.clipboard.writeText(text + '\\n\\nhttps://p10racing.app/predict');\n        showNotification('Picks copied to clipboard!', 'success');\n      }\n    }\n  };\n\n  if (authLoading || (!nextRace && loadingRace)) {\n    return <LoadingView />;\n  }\n\n  if (!session && !username) {\n    return (\n      <>\n        <Container className=\"mt-5\">\n          <Row className=\"justify-content-center\">\n            <Col md={5}>\n              <Card className=\"p-4 border-secondary shadow\">\n                <h2 className=\"h4 mb-4 fw-bold\">Who&apos;s Predicting?</h2>\n                <div className=\"mb-4\">\n                  <Link href=\"/auth\" passHref legacyBehavior><Button variant=\"danger\" className=\"w-100 py-3 fw-bold mb-2\">SIGN IN / CREATE ACCOUNT</Button></Link>\n                  <p className=\"text-center text-muted small mt-2\">OR PLAY AS GUEST (LOCAL ONLY)</p>\n                </div>\n                {existingPlayers.length > 0 && (\n                  <div className=\"mb-4\">\n                    <Form.Label className=\"text-muted small text-uppercase fw-semibold\">Recent Players</Form.Label>\n                    <div className=\"d-flex flex-wrap gap-2\">\n                      {existingPlayers.map(p => (\n                        <Button key={p} variant=\"outline-light\" size=\"sm\" onClick={() => selectUser(p)} className=\"rounded-pill px-3\">{p}</Button>\n                      ))}\n                    </div>\n                    <hr className=\"border-secondary mt-4\" />\n                  </div>\n                )}\n                <Form onSubmit={handleGuestLogin}>\n                  <Form.Group className=\"mb-3\"><Form.Label>Guest Name</Form.Label><Form.Control type=\"text\" placeholder=\"Enter name\" value={tempUsername} onChange={(e) => setTempUsername(e.target.value)} minLength={3} required className=\"bg-dark text-white border-secondary py-2\" /></Form.Group>\n                  <Button type=\"submit\" className=\"btn-f1 w-100 py-2 fw-bold\">CONTINUE AS GUEST</Button>\n                </Form>\n              </Card>\n            </Col>\n          </Row>\n        </Container>\n   }
}

(mountedRef.current) setLoading(false);\n      }\n    }\n    init();\n\n    // Listen for auth changes locally\n    const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange((_event,       } else {\n          setIsAdmin(false);\n        }\n      }\n    });\n\n    return () => {\n      subscription.unsubscribe();\n    };\n  }, [supabase]);\n  \n  const triggerHaptic = () => {\n    Haptics.impact({ style: ImpactStyle.Light });\n  };\n\n  const handleDeleteAccount = async () => {\n    if (!session) return;\n    setIsDeleting(true);\n    Haptics.notification({ type: NotificationType.Warning });\n    \n    try {\n      const { error } = await supabase.rpc('delete_user_data');\n      if (error) throw error;\n\n      await supabase.auth.signOut();\n Please try again.', 'error');\n      setIsDeleting(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  if (loading) {\n    return <LoadingView />;\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <>\n      <Container className=\"mt-4 mb-5 max-w-md mx-auto\" style={{ maxWidth: '600px' }}>\n        <h1 className=\"h4 fw-bold text-uppercase letter-spacing-1 mb-4 text-white ps-1\">Settings & Info</h1>\n\n        {isAdmin && (\n          <Card className=\"border-secondary border-opacity-25 shadow-sm bg-dark mb-4\">\n            <Link href=\"/admin\" passHref legacyBehavior>\n              <a className=\"text-decoration-none\" onClick={triggerHaptic}>\n                <Card.Body className=\"p-3 d-flex align-items-center justify-content-between cursor-pointer\">\n                  <div className=\"d-flex align-items-center\">\n                    <ShieldAlert size={20} className=\"text-warning opacity-75 me-3\" />\n                    <div>\n                      <h3 className=\"h6 mb-0 fw-bold text-white text-uppercase letter-spacing-1\">System Admin</h3>\n                      <p className=\"extra-small text-muted mb-0\">Race Results & Verification</p>\n                    </div>\n                  </div>\n                  <ChevronRight size={18} className=\"text-white opacity-25\" />\n                </Card.Body>\n              </a>\n            </Link>\n          </Card>\n        )}\n\n        <h2 className=\"small fw-bold text-uppercase text-muted letter-spacing-1 mb-2 ps-1\">Account</h2>\n        <Card className=\"border-secondary shadow-sm mb-4\">\n          <div className=\"list-group list-group-flush bg-dark rounded\">\n            {session ?  <div className=\"d-flex align-items-center\">\n                    <Trash2 size={18} className=\"me-3 opacity-75\" />\n                    <span className=\"fw-bold\">Delete Account Data</span>\n                  </div>\n                </button>\n              </>\n            ) : (\n              <div className=\"p-3 text-center text-muted small\">\n                Settings are limited while useState<string | null>(null);\n  const [status, setStatus] = useState<{message: string, variant: string} | null>(null);\n  const [showNotifyModal, setShowNotifyModal] = useState(false);\n  const const mountedRef = useRef(true);\n\n  // Lifecycle\n  useEffect(() => {\n    mountedRef.current = true;\n    return () => { mountedRef.current = false; };\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (status) {\n      const timer = setTimeout(() => setStatus(null), 5000);\n      return () => clearTimeout(timer);\n    }\n  }, [status]);\n\n  const checkExistingResults = useCallback(async () => {\n    if (!isAdmin || !selectedRace) return;\n    try {\n      const { data } = await withTimeout(supabase\n        .from('verified_results')\n        .select('data')\n        .eq('id', Object.entries(d.positions).find(([, pos]) => pos === 10)?.[0] || 'Unknown' : 'Unknown';\n        setExistingResult({ p10: p10Id, dnf: d.firstDnf || 'None' });\n      } else if (mountedRef.current) => {\n    checkExistingResults();\n  }, [checkExistingResults]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    async function initAuth() {\n      try {\n        const { data: { session: currentSession } } = await withTimeout(supabase.auth.getSession());\n        if (mountedRef.current) {\n          setSession(currentSession);\n          \n          if (!currentSession) {\n            router.push('/auth');\n            return;\n          }\n\n          const { data: profile } = await withTimeout(supabase\n            .from('profiles')\n            .select('is_admin')\n            .eq('id', load() {\n      setFirstDnf(''); \n      const d = await fetchDrivers(season);\n      if (mountedRef.current) {\n        if (d.length > 0) {\n          setDrivers(d);\n          setResults(Object.fromEntries(d.map((driver: Driver, i: number) => [driver.id, i + 1])));\n        } else {\n          setDrivers(FALLBACK_DRIVERS);\n          setResults(Object.fromEntries(FALLBACK_DRIVERS.map((driver, i) => [driver.id, i + 1])));\n        }\n      }\n\n      const cal = await fetchCalendar(season);\n      if (mountedRef.current) {\n        if (cal.length > 0) {\n          setAvailableRaces(cal);\n          setSelectedRace(cal[0].round);\n        } else {\n          setAvailableRaces(fallbackRaces);\n          setSelectedRace(fallbackRaces[0].round);\n        }\n        setLoading(false);\n      }\n    }\n    load();\n  }, [season, isAdmin, fallbackRaces]);\n\n  const handlePositionChange = (driverId: string, position: number) => {\n    setResults(prev => ({ ...prev, [driverId]: position }));\n  };\n\n  const handleFetchFromApi = async () => {\n    setLoading(true);\n    setError(null);\n    const raceInfo = availableRaces.find(r => r.round === selectedRace);\n    if (!raceInfo) {\n      setLoading(false);\n      return;\n    }\n\n    try {\n      const data = await fetchRaceResults(season, parseInt(raceInfo.round));\n      if (data && mountedRef.current) {\n        const participatingDrivers = data.Results.map(r => ({\n          id: r.Driver.driverId,\n          name: {\n          setFirstDnf('');\n        }\n        setStatus({ message: 'Data fetched successfully from API.', variant: 'success' });\n      } else {\n        setError(`No results found for Season ${season}, Round ${raceInfo.round}.`);\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error(err);\n      setError('Failed to fetch data from API.');\n    } finally {\n      if (mountedRef.current) message: `Results published! Open P10 Racing while connected to the internet to sync it before the race!',\n            id: notificationId,\n            schedule: { at: new Date(Date.now() + 1000 * 60 * 15) }\n          }\n        ]\n      });\n    }\n  } catch (err) {\n    console.log('Local Notifications not available', err);\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Atomic helper to remove from queue.\n */\nexport async function removeFromSyncQueue(raceId: string) {\n  const queue = getSyncQueue();\n  if (queue[raceId]) {\n    delete queue[raceId];\n    localStorage.setItem(QUEUE_KEY, JSON.stringify(queue));\n    try {\n      const { LocalNotifications } = await import('@capacitor/local-notifications');\n      const notificationId = parseInt(raceId.replace(/[^0-9]/g, '')) || Math.floor(Math.random() * 100000);\n      await LocalNotifications.cancel({ notifications: [{ id: notificationId }] });\n    } catch { /* ignore */ }\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Atomic helper to process the entire queue.\n */\nexport async function flushSyncQueue(\n  supabase: SupabaseClient, \n  onSuccess: (raceId: string) => void,\n  onLocked: (raceId: string) => void\n): Promise<number> {\n  const queue = getSyncQueue();\n  const raceIds = Object.keys(queue);\n  if (raceIds.length === 0) return 0;\n\n  let successCount = 0;\n  for (const raceId of raceIds) {\n    const payload = queue[raceId];\n    const { error } = await supabase.from('predictions').upsert(payload, { onConflict: 'user_id, race_id' });\n    \n    if (!error) {\n      await removeFromSyncQueue(raceId);\n      successCount++;\n      onSuccess(raceId);\n    } else if (error.message.includes('Predictions are locked')) {\n      await removeFromSyncQueue(raceId);\n      onLocked(raceId);\n    }\n  }\n  return successCount;\n}\n\n/**\n * Wraps a promise or thenable with a timeout.\n */\nexport async function withTimeout<T>(promise: Promise<T> | PromiseLike<T>, timeoutMs = 10000): Promise<T> {\n  let timeoutId: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | undefined;\n  \n  const timeoutPromise = new Promise<T>((_, reject) => {\n    timeoutId = setTimeout(() => {\n      console.warn(`Request timed out after ${timeoutMs}ms`);\n      reject(new Error('Request timed out'));\n    }, timeoutMs);\n  });\n\n  try {\n    const result = await Promise.race([promise, timeoutPromise]);\n    if (timeoutId) clearTimeout(timeoutId);\n    return result;\n  } catch (error) {\n    if (timeoutId) clearTimeout(timeoutId);\n    throw error;\n  }\n}\n"
  }
}

  "name": "write_file",

    "file_path": "components/AuthProvider.tsx",
    "content": "'use client';\n\nimport React, { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState, useCallback, useRef } from 'react';\nimport { createClient } from '@/lib/supabase/client';\nimport { Session, User } from '@supabase/supabase-js';\n\nexport interface Profile {\n  id: string;\n  username: string;\n  is_admin: boolean;\n  avatar_url?: string;\n}\n\ninterface AuthContextType {\n  session: Session | null;\n  user: User | null;\n  profile: Profile | null;\n  isLoading: boolean;\n}\n\nconst AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType>({\n  session: null,\n  user: null,\n  profile: null,\n  isLoading: true,\n});\n\n/**\n * A standard AuthProvider that syncs global auth state for UI reactivity.\n */\nexport function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {\n  const supabase = createClient();\n  const [session, setSession] = useState<Session | null>(null);\n  const [user, setUser] = useState<User | null>(null);\n  const [profile, setProfile] = useState<Profile | null>(null);\n  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);\n  const mountedRef = useRef(true);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    mountedRef.current = true;\n    return () => { mountedRef.current = false; };\n  }, []);\n\n  const fetchProfile = useCallback(async (userId: string) => {\n    try {\n      const { data, error } = await supabase\n        .from('profiles')\n        .select('id, username, is_admin, avatar_url')\n        .eq('id', userId)\n        .maybeSingle();\n      \n      if (error) throw error;\n\n      if (mountedRef.current) {\n        setProfile(data as Profile);\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('AuthProvider: Error fetching profile:', err);\n    }\n  }, [supabase]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    // 1. Initial Session Load\n    supabase.auth.getSession().then(({ data: { session: initialSession } }) => {\n      if (mountedRef.current) {\n        setSession(initialSession);\n        setUser(initialSession?.user ?? null);\n        if (initialSession?.user) {\n          fetchProfile(initialSession.user.id);\n        }\n        setIsLoading(false);\n      }\n    });\n\n    // 2. Listen for Auth Changes\n    const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange(async (_event, newSession) => {\n      if (mountedRef.current) {\n        setSession(newSession);\n        setUser(newSession?.user ?? null);\n        if (newSession?.user) {\n          await fetchProfile(newSession.user.id);\n        } else {\n          setProfile(null);\n        }\n        setIsLoading(false);\n      }\n    });\n\n    return () => {\n      subscription.unsubscribe();\n    };\n  }, [fetchProfile, supabase]);\n\n  return (\n    <AuthContext.Provider value={{ session, user, profile, isLoading }}>\n      {children}\n    </AuthContext.Provider>\n  );\n}\n\nexport function useAuth() {\n  const context = useContext(AuthContext);\n  if (context === undefined) {\n    throw new Error('useAuth must be used within an AuthProvider');\n  }\n  return context;\n}\n"

Here is the updated code:\n'use client';\n\nimport React, { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState, useCallback, useRef } from 'react';\nimport { createClient } from '@/lib/supabase/client';\nimport { Session, User } from '@supabase/supabase-js';\n\nexport interface Profile {\n  id: string;\n  username: string;\n  is_admin: boolean;\n  avatar_url?: string;\n}\n\ninterface AuthContextType {\n  session: Session | null;\n  user: User | null;\n  profile: Profile | null;\n  isLoading: boolean;\n}\n\nconst AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType>({\n  session: null,\n  user: null,\n  profile: null,\n  isLoading: true,\n});\n\n/**\n * A standard AuthProvider that syncs global auth state for UI reactivity.\n */\nexport function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {\n  const supabase = createClient();\n  const [session, setSession] = useState<Session | null>(null);\n  const [user, setUser] = useState<User | null>(null);\n  const [profile, setProfile] = useState<Profile | null>(null);\n  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);\n  const mountedRef = useRef(true);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    mountedRef.current = true;\n    return () => { mountedRef.current = false; };\n  }, []);\n\n  const fetchProfile = useCallback(async (userId: string) => {\n    try {\n      const { data, error } = await supabase\n        .from('profiles')\n        .select('id, username, is_admin, avatar_url')\n        .eq('id', userId)\n        .maybeSingle();\n      \n      if (error) throw error;\n\n      if (mountedRef.current) {\n        setProfile(data as Profile);\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('AuthProvider: Error fetching profile:', err);\n    }\n  }, [supabase]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    // 1. Initial Session Load\n    supabase.auth.getSession().then(({ data: { session: initialSession } }) => {\n      if (mountedRef.current) {\n        setSession(initialSession);\n        setUser(initialSession?.user ?? null);\n        if (initialSession?.user) {\n          fetchProfile(initialSession.user.id);\n        }\n        setIsLoading(false);\n      }\n    });\n\n    // 2. Listen for Auth Changes\n    const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange(async (_event, newSession) => {\n      if (mountedRef.current) {\n        setSession(newSession);\n        setUser(newSession?.user ?? null);\n        if (newSession?.user) {\n          await fetchProfile(newSession.user.id);\n        } else {\n          setProfile(null);\n        }\n        setIsLoading(false);\n      }\n    });\n\n    return () => {\n      subscription.unsubscribe();\n    };\n  }, [fetchProfile, supabase]);\n\n  return (\n    <AuthContext.Provider value={{ session, user, profile, isLoading }}>\n      {children}\n    </AuthContext.Provider>\n  );\n}\n\nexport function useAuth() {\n  const context = useContext(AuthContext);\n  if (context === undefined) {\n    throw new Error('useAuth must be used within an AuthProvider');\n  }\n  return context;\n}\n"
  }
}
